    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [PRMShapes] AS [p0] ON [t].[FKShapeId] = [p0].[ShapeId]
INNER JOIN [PRMProductCatalogueTypes] AS [p1] ON [t].[FKProductCatalogueTypeId] = [p1].[ProductCatalogueTypeId]
